morning
I've become inactive in the kpop world because of life. I was so active back in highschool but when I entered college, everything that I love suddenly just disappeared, like I don't have any passion for it anymore. Back in highschool, whenever I feel down or reviewing, I always listen to Apink. The wave was always my favorite to listen to when I feel down. And now that I'm in college and slowly transitioning to an adult, it's hard. Everything is just overwhelming. And today is my last day of exam for Midterms, I opened YouTube to search for something, then I saw Apink in the recommended section. I played it, took me back, and started crying. This song was exactly what I needed. It felt like I never left because they have always been with me the whole time. Thank you, Apink, for always healing my heart with your songs.
